(function($, ns) {
	$(function(){

		/* Hublot Timekeeper */
		function HublotTimekeeper(wrapper) {
			var _self = this;
			this.wrapper = wrapper;
			this.watchStarted = false;
			this.timerHours = this.wrapper.querySelector('#timer-hours');
			this.timerMinutes = this.wrapper.querySelector('#timer-minutes');

			this.initialize = function(){
				setTimeout(function(){
					window.setInterval(_self.update, 500);
				}, 500);
			};
			this.update = function(){
				var currentTime = new Date();
				if(!this.watchStarted)currentTime.setSeconds(currentTime.getSeconds() + 1);
				var h = currentTime.getHours(), m = currentTime.getMinutes(), s = currentTime.getSeconds(), ms = currentTime.getMilliseconds();
				
				h = h < 10 ? "0" + h : h;
				m = m < 10 ? "0" + m : m;
				_self.timerHours.innerHTML = h;
				_self.timerMinutes.innerHTML = m;
			};
		};

		$('.hublot-timekeeper').each(function() {
			var hublotTimekeeper = new HublotTimekeeper(this);
			hublotTimekeeper.initialize();
		});
	});
})(jQuery, window);
